### 

<span data-key="235c4776c1724f86aa9c514087e378ac"><span data-offset-key="235c4776c1724f86aa9c514087e378ac:0">Block-scoped variables</span></span>

<span data-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe"><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:0">When you are declaring a variable with the keyword </span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:4"> you are declaring a variable that exists within </span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">block scope</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:6">. Blocks in JavaScript are denoted by curly braces(</span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">{}</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:8">). The following examples create a block scope: </span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">if</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:10"> statements, </span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">while</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:12"> loops, </span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:13"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">switch</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:14"> statements, and </span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:15"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">for</span></span><span data-offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:16"> loops.</span></span>

<span data-key="d369c098a1d04f15a846b3a6c975fbf7"><span data-offset-key="d369c098a1d04f15a846b3a6c975fbf7:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Using the keyword let</span></span></span>

<span data-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd"><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:0">We can use </span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:2"> to declare </span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">re-assignable block-scoped variables</span></span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:4">. You are, of course, very familiar with </span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:6"> so let's take a look at how </span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:8"> works within a block scope:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362"><span data-offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">function</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">blockScope</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af"><span data-offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> test </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"upper scope"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

3

<span data-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2"><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">if</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">true</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be"><span data-offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> test </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"lower scope"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095"><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:0"> console</span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">test</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// "lower scope"</span></span></span></span></span>

6

<span data-key="93d2890dccd14dd682b7b8743a3c45d7"><span data-offset-key="93d2890dccd14dd682b7b8743a3c45d7:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="93d2890dccd14dd682b7b8743a3c45d7:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177"><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:0"> console</span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">test</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// "upper scope"</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="036b4bd3322345489c3ffc2f3f190357"><span data-offset-key="036b4bd3322345489c3ffc2f3f190357:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a"><span data-offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:0">In the example above we can see that the </span><span data-offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">test</span></span><span data-offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:2"> variable was declared twice using the keyword </span><span data-offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:4"> but since they were declared within different scopes they have different values.</span></span>

<span data-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43"><span data-offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:0">JavaScript will raise a </span><span data-offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">SyntaxError</span></span><span data-offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:2"> if you try to declare the same </span><span data-offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:4"> variable twice in one block.</span></span>

1

<span data-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229"><span data-offset-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">if</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">true</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="660a8fef357746ed8351c4cd90387229:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4"><span data-offset-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> test </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"this works!"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="fd5e28ba173e4339bdd03002f4512fd4:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc"><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> test </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"nope!"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ca388b0a4bc24d1bb3ce8e13193ac5bc:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// Identifier 'test' has already been declared</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="73f021fb81b745419b3430742c3d9e16"><span data-offset-key="73f021fb81b745419b3430742c3d9e16:0">Whereas if you try the same example with </span><span data-offset-key="73f021fb81b745419b3430742c3d9e16:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="73f021fb81b745419b3430742c3d9e16:2">:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="42e72baed75746399d0dbf7043274309"><span data-offset-key="42e72baed75746399d0dbf7043274309:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">var</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="42e72baed75746399d0dbf7043274309:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> test </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="42e72baed75746399d0dbf7043274309:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="42e72baed75746399d0dbf7043274309:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="42e72baed75746399d0dbf7043274309:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"this works!"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="42e72baed75746399d0dbf7043274309:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="c07117a827164645a194e44080755724"><span data-offset-key="c07117a827164645a194e44080755724:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">var</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c07117a827164645a194e44080755724:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> test </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c07117a827164645a194e44080755724:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c07117a827164645a194e44080755724:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c07117a827164645a194e44080755724:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"nope!"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c07117a827164645a194e44080755724:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

3

<span data-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc"><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:0">console</span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">test</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0a9acc851cf641848e9ba6c23012b4bc:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// prints "nope!"</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="3e81c9f832934c1681138f23c4d7722f"><span data-offset-key="3e81c9f832934c1681138f23c4d7722f:0">We can see above that </span><span data-offset-key="3e81c9f832934c1681138f23c4d7722f:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="3e81c9f832934c1681138f23c4d7722f:2"> will allow you to redeclare a variable twice which can lead to some very confusing and frustrating debugging.</span></span>

<span data-key="25586e7098234724bc8f9aa78dc73f64"><span data-offset-key="25586e7098234724bc8f9aa78dc73f64:0">Feel free to peruse the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/let" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406" data-rnw-int-class="257-15655_259-15656-237__"><span data-key="63cbeefa3dff4d3da6bef8a2b959291e"><span data-offset-key="63cbeefa3dff4d3da6bef8a2b959291e:0">documentation</span></span></span></a><span data-key="016cd0bb7f874277b35ee6d94890a7ff"><span data-offset-key="016cd0bb7f874277b35ee6d94890a7ff:0"> for the keyword </span><span data-offset-key="016cd0bb7f874277b35ee6d94890a7ff:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="016cd0bb7f874277b35ee6d94890a7ff:2"> for more examples.</span></span>

<span data-key="ab6ab002bf7647e5b79c66c0c8bab99f"><span data-offset-key="ab6ab002bf7647e5b79c66c0c8bab99f:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Using the keyword const</span></span></span>

<span data-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36"><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:0">We use </span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:2"> to declare </span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">block-scoped variables</span></span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:4"> that can </span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">not</span></span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:6"> be reassigned. In JavaScript variables that cannot be reassigned are called </span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">constants</span></span><span data-offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:8">. Constants should be used for values that will not be re-declared or re-assigned.</span></span>

<span data-key="5f72a819ac044bde8141d1cf8cb9ed36"><span data-offset-key="5f72a819ac044bde8141d1cf8cb9ed36:0">Properties of constants:</span></span>

<span data-key="8cd6513e41ba45579da48cbd281d1220"><span data-offset-key="8cd6513e41ba45579da48cbd281d1220:0">Let's look at a quick example of what happens when trying to reassign a constant:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb"><span data-offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">&gt;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao <span data-key="fef63b212aee4c6184a2f1e3ffcb5b69"><span data-offset-key="fef63b212aee4c6184a2f1e3ffcb5b69:0">Constants cannot be reassigned but, just like with </span><span data-offset-key="fef63b212aee4c6184a2f1e3ffcb5b69:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="fef63b212aee4c6184a2f1e3ffcb5b69:2">, new constants of the same names can be declared within nested scopes.</span></span>

<span data-key="2b915b62ce6c4fe9a91bde646b8e25d0"><span data-offset-key="2b915b62ce6c4fe9a91bde646b8e25d0:0">Take a look at the following for an example:</span></span>

<span data-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64"><span data-offset-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">if</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">true</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="56757374feea43eaaa0afae42cd9ce64:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="10b3f06018944da5bf31eccea9171520"><span data-offset-key="10b3f06018944da5bf31eccea9171520:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="47e134acd62540ac964fa18dcb2df21b"><span data-offset-key="47e134acd62540ac964fa18dcb2df21b:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Hoisting with block-scoped variables</span></span></span>

<span data-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8"><span data-offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:0">When JavaScript ES6 introduced new ways of declaring a variable using </span><span data-offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:4"> the idea of block-level hoisting was also introduced. Block scope hoisting allows developers to avoid previous debugging debacles that naturally happened from using </span><span data-offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:6">.</span></span>

<span data-key="00e955ce10db45098c338205ab59bcae"><span data-offset-key="00e955ce10db45098c338205ab59bcae:0">Let's take a look at what hoisting does to a </span><span data-offset-key="00e955ce10db45098c338205ab59bcae:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">block-scoped</span></span><span data-offset-key="00e955ce10db45098c338205ab59bcae:2"> variable:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534"><span data-offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">if</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">true</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae"><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:0"> console</span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">str</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// =&gt; Uncaught ReferenceError: Cannot access 'str' before initialization</span></span></span></span></span>

3

<span data-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50"><span data-offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">const</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> str </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"apple"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

4

<span data-key="309b76a56b934e9aaa9f394c432022dc"><span data-offset-key="309b76a56b934e9aaa9f394c432022dc:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="72560b76ede5446690ae9c614d26b8a3"><span data-offset-key="72560b76ede5446690ae9c614d26b8a3:0">Looking at the above we can see that an explicit error is thrown if you attempt to use a block-scoped variable before it was declared. This is the typical behavior in a lot of programming languages - that a variable cannot be referred to until initialized to a value.</span></span>

<span data-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7"><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:0">However, JavaScript is still performing hoisting with block-scoped declared variables. The difference lies is how it </span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">initializes</span></span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:2"> them. Meaning that </span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:6"> variables are </span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">not</span></span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:8"> initialized to the value of </span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">undefined</span></span><span data-offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:10">.</span></span>

<span data-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232"><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:0">The time before a </span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:4"> variable is declared, but not used is called the </span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">Temporal Dead Zone</span></span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:6">. A very cool name for a simple idea. Variables declared using </span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:8"> and </span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:10"> are not initialized until their definitions are evaluated. Meaning, you will get an error if you try to reference a </span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:12"> or </span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:13"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:14"> declared variable before it is evaluated.</span></span>

<span data-key="926775206ae64c39ae9f6a92aa4c2f1c"><span data-offset-key="926775206ae64c39ae9f6a92aa4c2f1c:0">Let's look at one more example that should illuminate the presence of the </span><span data-offset-key="926775206ae64c39ae9f6a92aa4c2f1c:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">Temporal Dead Zone</span></span><span data-offset-key="926775206ae64c39ae9f6a92aa4c2f1c:2">:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5"><span data-offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">var</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> str </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"not apple"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="3c83d43021ec4bcb8a5a14ee8ae59164"><span data-offset-key="3c83d43021ec4bcb8a5a14ee8ae59164:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

3

<span data-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d"><span data-offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">if</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">true</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

4

<span data-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da"><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:0"> console</span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">str</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">//Uncaught ReferenceError: Cannot access 'str' before initialization</span></span></span></span></span>

5

<span data-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70"><span data-offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> str </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"apple"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

6

<span data-key="419f701af4374ac387b008db827c1457"><span data-offset-key="419f701af4374ac387b008db827c1457:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c"><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:0">In the above example we can see that inside the </span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">if</span></span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:2"> block the </span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:4"> declared variable, </span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">str</span></span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:6">, throws an error. Showing that the error thrown by a </span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:8"> variable in the temporal dead zone takes precedence over any scope chaining that would attempt to go to the outer scope to find a value for the </span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">str</span></span><span data-offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:10"> variable.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="2a948523cf1a4c6a8ea723ad39af4f7c"><span data-offset-key="2a948523cf1a4c6a8ea723ad39af4f7c:0">Function scope vs. block scope</span></span>

<span data-key="4c9daa75736d462ea22cde964824e00d"><span data-offset-key="4c9daa75736d462ea22cde964824e00d:0">Let's now take a deeper look at the comparison of using function vs. block scoped variables.</span></span>

<span data-key="389fc22b6224456c818f80e149227459"><span data-offset-key="389fc22b6224456c818f80e149227459:0">Let's start with a simple example:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7"><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:0"> console</span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"this is a "</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">+</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> string</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c2b6a46222e7436493669217b8cf54e7:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="f2f95461c4b44442a6b52d220818cf01"><span data-offset-key="f2f95461c4b44442a6b52d220818cf01:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

13

<span data-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5"><span data-offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">partyMachine</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// =&gt; "this is a bummer"</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230"><span data-offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:0">We can see in the above example how the flexibility of </span><span data-offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:2"> can ultimately be a bad thing. Since </span><span data-offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:4"> is function-scoped </span><span data-offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">and</span></span><span data-offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:6"> can be reassigned and re-declared without error it is very easy to overwrite variable values by accident.</span></span>

<span data-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07"><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:0">This is the problem that ES6 introduced </span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:4"> to solve. Since </span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:6"> and </span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:8"> are block-scoped it's a lot easier to avoid accidentally overwriting variable values.</span></span>

<span data-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d"><span data-offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:0">Let's take a look at the example function above rewritten using </span><span data-offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:4">:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04"><span data-offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">function</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">partyMachine</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="7075164225654c458ff9aed143a19b79"><span data-offset-key="7075164225654c458ff9aed143a19b79:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">partyMachine</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="7075164225654c458ff9aed143a19b79:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="7075164225654c458ff9aed143a19b79:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="7075164225654c458ff9aed143a19b79:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="7075164225654c458ff9aed143a19b79:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="7075164225654c458ff9aed143a19b79:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// =&gt; "this is a party"</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="b9da14908b6e4384a6b9880f8f38f0ca"><span data-offset-key="b9da14908b6e4384a6b9880f8f38f0ca:0">Global variables</span></span>

<span data-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd"><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:0">If you leave off a declaration when initializing a variable, it will become a global. </span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Do not do this.</span></span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:2"> We declare variables using the keywords </span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">var</span></span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">let</span></span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:6">, and </span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">const</span></span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:8"> to ensure that our variables are declared within a proper scope. Any variables declared without these keywords will be declared on the </span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">global scope</span></span><span data-offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:10">.</span></span>

<span data-key="a6c08295880a42e98c543adf06acdbd2"><span data-offset-key="a6c08295880a42e98c543adf06acdbd2:0">JavaScript has a single global scope, which means all of the files from your projects and any libraries you use will </span><span data-offset-key="a6c08295880a42e98c543adf06acdbd2:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">all be sharing the same scope</span></span><span data-offset-key="a6c08295880a42e98c543adf06acdbd2:2">. Every time a variable is declared on the global scope, the chance of a name collision increases. If we are unaware of the global variables in our code, we may accidentally overwrite variables.</span></span>

<span data-key="6c3de8e9916a459a885b31bc98d8a487"><span data-offset-key="6c3de8e9916a459a885b31bc98d8a487:0">Let's look at a quick example showing why this is a bad idea:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe"><span data-offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">function</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">good</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8"><span data-offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> x </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">5</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

3

<span data-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105"><span data-offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> y </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"yay"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9"><span data-offset-key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">why</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="f2b6f19a1f804cef97f0a32dfdc38090"><span data-offset-key="f2b6f19a1f804cef97f0a32dfdc38090:0">Limiting global variables will help you create code that is much more easily maintainable. Strive to write your functions so that they are self-contained and not reliant on outside variables. This will also be a huge help in allowing us test each function by itself.</span></span>

<span data-key="ca7ee29bfcbe4a11a693c9399ed0ecbf"><span data-offset-key="ca7ee29bfcbe4a11a693c9399ed0ecbf:0">One of our jobs as programmers is to write code that can be integrated easily within a team. In order to do that, we need to limit the number of globally declared variables in our code as much as possible, to avoid accidental name collisions.</span></span>

<span data-key="f1508c6e4ea7498589a08f0c12860ba0"><span data-offset-key="f1508c6e4ea7498589a08f0c12860ba0:0">Sloppy programmers use global variables, and you are not working so hard in order to be a sloppy programmer!</span></span>

<span data-key="4449dfc8d38f4074884df48b45931b31"><span data-offset-key="4449dfc8d38f4074884df48b45931b31:0">dentify the different ways to declare a variable in JavaScript</span></span>

<span data-key="ce9e3e589130415ea2c6ca656a70313c"><span data-offset-key="ce9e3e589130415ea2c6ca656a70313c:0">Calculating Closures</span></span>

<span data-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a"><span data-offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:0">What is a </span><span data-offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">closure</span></span><span data-offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:2">? This question is one of the </span><span data-offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">most frequent interview questions</span></span><span data-offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:4"> where JavaScript is involved. If you answer this question quickly and knowledgeably you'll look like a great candidate. We know you want to know it all so let's dive right in!</span></span>

<span data-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58"><span data-offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:0">The official definition of a closure from MDN is, "A closure is the combination of a function and the lexical environment within which that function was declared." The practicality of how a </span><span data-offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">closure</span></span><span data-offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:2"> is used it simple: a </span><span data-offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">closure</span></span><span data-offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:4"> is when an inner function uses, or changes, variables in an outer function. Closures in JavaScript are incredibly important in terms of the creativity, flexibility and security of your code.</span></span>

<span data-key="eb81419b041b446383fedecf3789858b"><span data-offset-key="eb81419b041b446383fedecf3789858b:0">When you finish this reading you should be able to implement a closure and explain how that closure effects scope.</span></span>

<span data-key="d1528ddb66e84326a4222ad886d9c2c1"><span data-offset-key="d1528ddb66e84326a4222ad886d9c2c1:0">Closures and scope</span></span>

<span data-key="d3623422e7b049c893ffb74899332e42"><span data-offset-key="d3623422e7b049c893ffb74899332e42:0">Let's look at an example of a simple closure below:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3"><span data-offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> treeString </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"You climbed a "</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe"><span data-offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:0">In the above snippet the </span><span data-offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">sayClimbTree</span></span><span data-offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:2"> function captures and uses the </span><span data-offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">treeString</span></span><span data-offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">treeType</span></span><span data-offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:6"> variables within its own inner scope.</span></span>

<span data-key="35698b34d9a44b508e20fc22af5841ee"><span data-offset-key="35698b34d9a44b508e20fc22af5841ee:0">Let's go over some basic closure rules:</span></span>

<span data-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f"><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:0">Notice above that even though the above </span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">climbTree</span></span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:2"> had run its </span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">return</span></span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:4"> statement the inner function of </span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">sayClimbTree</span></span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:6"> </span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">still has access</span></span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:8"> to the variables(</span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">treeString</span></span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:10"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">treeType</span></span><span data-offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:12">) from the outer scope where it was declared. So, even after an outer function has returned, an inner function will still have access to the outer functionâ€™s variables.</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3"><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:0">In the above example the function the anonymous function within the </span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">makeAdder</span></span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:2"> function </span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">closes over</span></span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:4"> the </span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">x</span></span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:6"> variable and utilizes it within the inner anonymous function. This allows us to do some pretty cool stuff like creating the </span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">add5</span></span><span data-offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:8"> function above. Closures are your friend â¤ï¸.</span></span>

<span data-key="f4cab43a4343499cb09199ffc10e5b83"><span data-offset-key="f4cab43a4343499cb09199ffc10e5b83:0">Applications of closures</span></span>

<span data-key="1d25fb60dccf42e7bfe3832e9bda8975"><span data-offset-key="1d25fb60dccf42e7bfe3832e9bda8975:0">Let's take a look at some of the common and practical applications of closures in JavaScript.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="0d81030b71154108a6e76810229e4a87"><span data-offset-key="0d81030b71154108a6e76810229e4a87:0">Private State</span></span>

<span data-key="31d9ba03e8124f0db4e2094572f69707"><span data-offset-key="31d9ba03e8124f0db4e2094572f69707:0">Information hiding is incredibly important in the world of software engineering. JavaScript as a language does not have a way of declaring a function as exclusively private, as can be done in other programming languages. We can however, use </span><span data-offset-key="31d9ba03e8124f0db4e2094572f69707:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">closures</span></span><span data-offset-key="31d9ba03e8124f0db4e2094572f69707:2"> to create private state within a function.</span></span>

<span data-key="0e67631ed6754e47a67fa7ea4ec893de"><span data-offset-key="0e67631ed6754e47a67fa7ea4ec893de:0">The following code illustrates how to use </span><span data-offset-key="0e67631ed6754e47a67fa7ea4ec893de:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">closures</span></span><span data-offset-key="0e67631ed6754e47a67fa7ea4ec893de:2"> to define functions that can emulate private functions and variables:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1"><span data-offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">function</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">createCounter</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>
