Copied!

<span data-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea"><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:0">In the above code we are storing the anonymous inner function inside the </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">createCounter</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:2"> function onto the variable </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">counter</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:4">. The </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">counter</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:6"> variable is now a </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">closure</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:8">. The </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">counter</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:10"> variable </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">closes over</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:12"> the inner </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:13"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">count</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:14"> value inside </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:15"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">createCounter</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:16"> even after </span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:17"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">createCounter</span></span><span data-offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:18"> has returned.</span></span>

<span data-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7"><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:0">By </span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">closing over</span></span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:2"> (or </span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">capturing</span></span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:4">) the </span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">count</span></span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:6"> variable, each function that is return from </span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">createCounter</span></span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:8"> has a </span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">private</span></span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:10">, mutable state that cannot be accessed externally. There is no way any outside function beside the closure itself can access the </span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">count</span></span><span data-offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:12"> state.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="cae41ae986494a13bedfb63bd08629e9"><span data-offset-key="cae41ae986494a13bedfb63bd08629e9:0">Passing Arguments Implicitly</span></span>

<span data-key="62a3ed7f318241809c960ed597df6d30"><span data-offset-key="62a3ed7f318241809c960ed597df6d30:0">We can use closures to pass down arguments to helper functions without explicitly passing them into that helper function.</span></span>

<span data-key="a549bfc600ed45c68cdc27ffae248cdd"><span data-offset-key="a549bfc600ed45c68cdc27ffae248cdd:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="a549bfc600ed45c68cdc27ffae248cdd:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="a549bfc600ed45c68cdc27ffae248cdd:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">reverse</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="a549bfc600ed45c68cdc27ffae248cdd:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="a549bfc600ed45c68cdc27ffae248cdd:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74"><span data-offset-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">join</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">""</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f95c250b6c404deba4b9b4b215c23a74:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="d8d858fb9ac547d0bab4c5c5a0107ee4"><span data-offset-key="d8d858fb9ac547d0bab4c5c5a0107ee4:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="d8d858fb9ac547d0bab4c5c5a0107ee4:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="0be040ed975d473d9aad7b3f99029424"><span data-offset-key="0be040ed975d473d9aad7b3f99029424:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span data-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d"><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">return</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> string </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">===</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">reverse</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c56d2a0fbd2f437c84a050207a500a7d:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

10

<span data-key="5aeb25be67ed4b50909829571323c079"><span data-offset-key="5aeb25be67ed4b50909829571323c079:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="4d8529c7aae74d6fa032f42ae2911cac"><span data-offset-key="4d8529c7aae74d6fa032f42ae2911cac:0">How to implement a closure and explain how that closure effects scope.</span></span>

<span data-key="84bea68b8a274ea29ab5d261d7030a0a"><span data-offset-key="84bea68b8a274ea29ab5d261d7030a0a:0">Context in JavaScript</span></span>

<span data-key="d31c679239fe4a01b0d85d3d0edaaee8"><span data-offset-key="d31c679239fe4a01b0d85d3d0edaaee8:0">It's now time to dive into one of the most interesting concepts in JavaScript: the idea of </span><span data-offset-key="d31c679239fe4a01b0d85d3d0edaaee8:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">context</span></span><span data-offset-key="d31c679239fe4a01b0d85d3d0edaaee8:2">.</span></span>

<span data-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea"><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:0">Programmers from the junior to senior level often confuse </span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">scope</span></span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">context</span></span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:4"> as the same thing - but that is not the case! Every function that is invoked has </span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">both</span></span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:6"> a scope and a context associated with that function. </span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">Scope</span></span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:8"> refers to the visibility and availability of variables, whereas </span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">context</span></span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:10"> refers to the value of the </span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:12"> keyword when code is executed.</span></span>

<span data-key="f7a0a42446a2465aa79a9f0e0ac3be15"><span data-offset-key="f7a0a42446a2465aa79a9f0e0ac3be15:0">When you finish this reading you should be able to:</span></span>

<span data-key="d8a54444406d45d994d31cb5ffc79331"><span data-offset-key="d8a54444406d45d994d31cb5ffc79331:0">What about </span><span data-offset-key="d8a54444406d45d994d31cb5ffc79331:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="d8a54444406d45d994d31cb5ffc79331:2">?</span></span>

<span data-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125"><span data-offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:0">When learning about objects we previously came across the idea of a </span><span data-offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">method</span></span><span data-offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:2">. A </span><span data-offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">method</span></span><span data-offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:4"> is a function that is a value within an object and belongs to an object.</span></span>

<span data-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e"><span data-offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:0">There will be times when you will have to know which object a method belongs to. The keyword </span><span data-offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:2"> exists in every function and it evaluates to the object that is currently invoking that function. So the value of </span><span data-offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:4"> relies entirely on </span><span data-offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">where</span></span><span data-offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:6"> a function is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-key="6dc73db04aba41c1917f38c1bb7bec93"><span data-offset-key="6dc73db04aba41c1917f38c1bb7bec93:0">That may sound pretty abstract, so let's jump into an example:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d"><span data-offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> dog </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="880fc559f17a48ba8dc1c208e580e55f"><span data-offset-key="880fc559f17a48ba8dc1c208e580e55f:0"> name</span><span data-offset-key="880fc559f17a48ba8dc1c208e580e55f:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">:</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="880fc559f17a48ba8dc1c208e580e55f:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="880fc559f17a48ba8dc1c208e580e55f:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"Bowser"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="880fc559f17a48ba8dc1c208e580e55f:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">,</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d"><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:0">Inside of a method, we can use the keyword </span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:2"> to refer to the object that is calling that method! So when calling </span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">dog.stand()</span></span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:4"> and we invoke the code of the </span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">stand</span></span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:6"> method, </span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:8"> will refer to the </span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">dog</span></span><span data-offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:10"> object.</span></span>

<span data-key="230a109c617942d680a0b3fa049ca4c1"><span data-offset-key="230a109c617942d680a0b3fa049ca4c1:0">Still skeptical? <span data-key="abffbba0197c4af9aad0c0379acfbea4"><span data-offset-key="abffbba0197c4af9aad0c0379acfbea4:0">In short, by using the </span><span data-offset-key="abffbba0197c4af9aad0c0379acfbea4:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="abffbba0197c4af9aad0c0379acfbea4:2"> keyword inside a method, we can refer to values within that object.</span></span>

<span data-key="bae02a715a4d469187f11bc67a691b7a"><span data-offset-key="bae02a715a4d469187f11bc67a691b7a:0">Let's look at another example of this:</span></span>

<span data-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055"><span data-offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:0">cat</span><span data-offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">purrMore</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed"><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:0">Through the </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:2"> variable, the </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:4"> method can access the object it was called on. In </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:6">, we use </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:8"> to access the </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">cat</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:10"> object that has a </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purr</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:12"> method. In other words, inside of the </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:13"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:14"> function if we had tried to use </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:15"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purr()</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:16"> instead of </span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:17"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this.purr()</span></span><span data-offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:18"> it would not work.</span></span>

<span data-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34"><span data-offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:0">When we invoked the </span><span data-offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:2"> function using </span><span data-offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">cat.purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:4"> we used a </span><span data-offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">method-style</span></span><span data-offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:6"> invocation.</span></span>

<span data-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2"><span data-offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:0">Method style invocations follow the format: </span><span data-offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">object.method(args)</span></span><span data-offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:2">. You've already been doing this using built in data type methods! (i.e. </span><span data-offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">Array\#push</span></span><span data-offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">String\#toUpperCase</span></span><span data-offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:6">, etc.)</span></span>

<span data-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8"><span data-offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">method-style invocation</span></span><span data-offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:2"> (note the </span><span data-offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">dot notation</span></span><span data-offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:4">) ensures the method will be invoked and that the </span><span data-offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:6"> within the method will be the object that method was called upon.</span></span>

<span data-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6"><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:0">Now that we have gone over what </span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:2"> refers to - you can have a full understanding of the definition of context. </span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Context refers to the value of </span></span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span></span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q"> within a function and </span></span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span></span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q"> refers to where a function is invoked</span></span><span data-offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:8">.</span></span>

<span data-key="29072a9642524ef783546e1a1ccf97f9"><span data-offset-key="29072a9642524ef783546e1a1ccf97f9:0">Issues with scope and context</span></span>

<span data-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2"><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:0">In the case of context the value of </span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:2"> is determined by </span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">how</span></span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:4"> a function is invoked. In the above section we talked briefly about </span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">method-style invocation</span></span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:6">, where </span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:8"> is set to the object the method was called upon.</span></span>

<span data-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce"><span data-offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:0">Let's now talk about what </span><span data-offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:2"> is when using normal </span><span data-offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">function style invocation</span></span><span data-offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:4">.</span></span>

<span data-key="984480e2dda54236a8d12520fa7c3392"><span data-offset-key="984480e2dda54236a8d12520fa7c3392:0">If you run the following in Node:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1"><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:0"> console</span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">this</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">//</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512"><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:0">When you run the above </span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">testMe</span></span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:2"> function in Node you'll see that </span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:4"> is set to the </span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">global</span></span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:6"> object. To reiterate: each function you invoke will have </span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">both</span></span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:8"> a context and a scope. So even running functions in Node that are not defined explicitly on declared objects are run using the global object as their </span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:10"> and therefore their context.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="fb043653e1a240408a57b296fd899d3e"><span data-offset-key="fb043653e1a240408a57b296fd899d3e:0">When methods have an unexpected context</span></span>

<span data-key="3d4185907b3147ef9607439ede3a5d32"><span data-offset-key="3d4185907b3147ef9607439ede3a5d32:0">So let's now look at what happens when we try to invoke a method using an unintended context.</span></span>

<span data-key="02894c8c9a4647ecbd244adcd7b83625"><span data-offset-key="02894c8c9a4647ecbd244adcd7b83625:0">Say we have a function that will change the name of a dog object:</span></span>

<span data-key="419f0d61acf847109cbbfac85fe2e0f6"><span data-offset-key="419f0d61acf847109cbbfac85fe2e0f6:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="419f0d61acf847109cbbfac85fe2e0f6:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> dog </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="419f0d61acf847109cbbfac85fe2e0f6:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="419f0d61acf847109cbbfac85fe2e0f6:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="419f0d61acf847109cbbfac85fe2e0f6:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="0053ff09069f4c5b8313751784680375"><span data-offset-key="0053ff09069f4c5b8313751784680375:0"> name</span><span data-offset-key="0053ff09069f4c5b8313751784680375:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">:</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0053ff09069f4c5b8313751784680375:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0053ff09069f4c5b8313751784680375:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"Bowser"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0053ff09069f4c5b8313751784680375:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">,</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="3f94c3b93af74cf7a388516486b92b18"><span data-offset-key="3f94c3b93af74cf7a388516486b92b18:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">}</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="3f94c3b93af74cf7a388516486b92b18:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="7a4bd5ee4fed41bab1615e2ea4c1f9ff"><span data-offset-key="7a4bd5ee4fed41bab1615e2ea4c1f9ff:0">Now say we wanted to take the </span><span data-offset-key="7a4bd5ee4fed41bab1615e2ea4c1f9ff:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">changeName</span></span><span data-offset-key="7a4bd5ee4fed41bab1615e2ea4c1f9ff:2"> function above and call it somewhere else. Maybe we have a callback we'd like to pass it to or another object or something like that.</span></span>

<span data-key="cafc1209a48746ff8d3beb2d00ddee1e"><span data-offset-key="cafc1209a48746ff8d3beb2d00ddee1e:0">Let's take a look at what happens when we try to isolate and invoke just the </span><span data-offset-key="cafc1209a48746ff8d3beb2d00ddee1e:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">changeName</span></span><span data-offset-key="cafc1209a48746ff8d3beb2d00ddee1e:2"> function:</span></span>

<span data-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118"><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:0">console</span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">this</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1866fbc6175c4016ae809bd8efa71118:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// Object \[global\] {etc, etc, etc, name: 'Layla'}</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3"><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:0">So in the above code notice how we stored the </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">dog.changeName</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:2"> function </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">without invoking it</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:4"> to the variable </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">change</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:6">. On the next line when we did invoke the </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">change</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:8"> function we can see that we did not actually change the </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">dog</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:10"> object like we intended to. We created a new key value pair for </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">name</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:12"> on the global object! This is because we invoked change without the context of a specific object (like </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:13"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">dog</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:14">), so JavaScript used the only object available to it, the </span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:15"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">global object</span></span><span data-offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:16">!</span></span>

<span data-key="5645127e2fa5408f8c2592c9c3752500"><span data-offset-key="5645127e2fa5408f8c2592c9c3752500:0">The above example might seem like an annoying inconvenience but let's take a look at what happens when calling something in the wrong context can be a big problem.</span></span>

<span data-key="060f5f98ccf947ee82558c24ade39db7"><span data-offset-key="060f5f98ccf947ee82558c24ade39db7:0">Using our </span><span data-offset-key="060f5f98ccf947ee82558c24ade39db7:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">cat</span></span><span data-offset-key="060f5f98ccf947ee82558c24ade39db7:2"> object from before:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="05e089c447eb410f99b2d79327f9e494"><span data-offset-key="05e089c447eb410f99b2d79327f9e494:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="05e089c447eb410f99b2d79327f9e494:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> cat </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="05e089c447eb410f99b2d79327f9e494:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="05e089c447eb410f99b2d79327f9e494:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="05e089c447eb410f99b2d79327f9e494:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d"><span data-offset-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> notACat </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> cat</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">purrMore</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="15f1e4508adb44f7be2c975477313b3d:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

11

<span data-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163"><span data-offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:0">console</span><span data-offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:1"><span data-offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">log</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:8"><span class="css-901oao class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:10"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// TypeError: this.purr is not a function</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944"><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:0">So in the above code snippet we attempted to call the </span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:2"> function </span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">without the correct Object for context</span></span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:4">. Meaning we attempted to call the </span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:6"> function on the global object! Since the global object does not have a </span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purr</span></span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:8"> method upon its </span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:10"> it raised an error. This is a common problem when invoking methods: invoking methods without their proper context.</span></span>

<span data-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b"><span data-offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:0">Let's look at one more example of confusing </span><span data-offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:2"> when using a callback. Incorrectly passing context is an inherent problem with callbacks. The </span><span data-offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">global.setTimeout()</span></span><span data-offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:4"> method on the global object is a popular way of setting a function to run on a timer. The </span><span data-offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">global.setTimeout()</span></span><span data-offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:6"> method accepts a callback and a number of milliseconds to wait before invoking the callback.</span></span>

<span data-key="992088c417594723b8c6be76f56793b7"><span data-offset-key="992088c417594723b8c6be76f56793b7:0">Let's look at a simple example:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb"><span data-offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">hello</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:6"><span class="css-901oao <span data-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52"><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:0">So what happened there? We called </span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">cat.purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:2"> so it should have the right context right? Noooooope. This is because </span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">cat.purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:4"> is a callback in the above code! Meaning that when the </span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">global.setTimeout</span></span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:6"> function attempts to call the </span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:8"> function all it has reference to is the function itself. Since </span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">setTimeout</span></span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:10"> is on the global object that means that the global object will be the context for attempting to invoke the </span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">cat.purrMore</span></span><span data-offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:12"> function.</span></span>

<span data-key="182024cf98aa480bac3e3e690d307c11"><span data-offset-key="182024cf98aa480bac3e3e690d307c11:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Strictly protecting the global object</span></span></span>

<span data-key="bb5187066bbe4da7aca2f1a87758259e"><span data-offset-key="bb5187066bbe4da7aca2f1a87758259e:0">The accidental mutation of the global object when invoking functions in unintended contexts is one of the reasons JavaScript released "strict" mode in ECMAScript version 5. We won't dive too much into JavaScript's strict mode here, but it's important to know how strict mode can be used to protect the global object.</span></span>

<span data-key="fb4ca22e82e444b9a33100bb89c85f84"><span data-offset-key="fb4ca22e82e444b9a33100bb89c85f84:0">Writing and running code in strict mode is easy and much like writing code in "sloppy mode" (jargon for the normal JavaScript environment). We can run JavaScript in strict mode simply by adding the string "use strict" at the top of our file:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="2c40a1b4f72f4613870149965548753d"><span data-offset-key="2c40a1b4f72f4613870149965548753d:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"use strict"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="2c40a1b4f72f4613870149965548753d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="4743e2bbe5684b3cad8e85d5a6cddde3"><span data-offset-key="4743e2bbe5684b3cad8e85d5a6cddde3:0">One of the differences of strict mode becomes apparent when trying to access the global object. As we mentioned previously, the global object is the context of invoked functions in Node that are not defined explicitly on declared objects.</span></span>

<span data-key="fbda9b7372274006973708a18da3a169"><span data-offset-key="fbda9b7372274006973708a18da3a169:0">So referencing </span><span data-offset-key="fbda9b7372274006973708a18da3a169:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="fbda9b7372274006973708a18da3a169:2"> within a function using the global object as its context will give us access to the global object:</span></span>

<span data-key="287b24faa8c541df8afbd61036e4cf2b"><span data-offset-key="287b24faa8c541df8afbd61036e4cf2b:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">hello</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="287b24faa8c541df8afbd61036e4cf2b:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="287b24faa8c541df8afbd61036e4cf2b:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="287b24faa8c541df8afbd61036e4cf2b:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="287b24faa8c541df8afbd61036e4cf2b:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="287b24faa8c541df8afbd61036e4cf2b:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// Object \[global\] {etc, etc, etc }</span></span></span></span></span>

<span data-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b"><span data-offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:0">However, strict mode will no longer allow you access to the global object in functions via the </span><span data-offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:2"> keyword and will instead return </span><span data-offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">undefined</span></span><span data-offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:4">:</span></span>

13

<span data-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c"><span data-offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:0">console</span><span data-offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:10"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// TypeError: Cannot set property 'name' of undefined</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9"><span data-offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:0">As you can see above, when we attempt to invoke the </span><span data-offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">changeNameFunc</span></span><span data-offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:2"> an error is thrown because referencing </span><span data-offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:4"> in strict mode will give us </span><span data-offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">undefined</span></span><span data-offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:6"> instead of the global object. The above behavior is helpful for catching otherwise tricky bugs.</span></span>

<span data-key="104951bc79c34c3aa86daeaecea1c6e3"><span data-offset-key="104951bc79c34c3aa86daeaecea1c6e3:0">If you'd like to learn more about strict mode we recommend checking out the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Strict_mode" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406" data-rnw-int-class="257-15655_259-15656-237__"><span data-key="15010c68c46c4df98e80004e1dbaeca4"><span data-offset-key="15010c68c46c4df98e80004e1dbaeca4:0">documentation</span></span></span></a><span data-key="e21dbce6c7fe4ba8bdbab11ca12e35dc"><span data-offset-key="e21dbce6c7fe4ba8bdbab11ca12e35dc:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="a050a676b272402abe50e3eab15d97aa"><span data-offset-key="a050a676b272402abe50e3eab15d97aa:0">Changing context using </span><span data-offset-key="a050a676b272402abe50e3eab15d97aa:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span></span>

<span data-key="220d3a6246434594b642d9ec25a3fcb7"><span data-offset-key="220d3a6246434594b642d9ec25a3fcb7:0">Good thing JavaScript has something that can solve this problem for us: what is known as the </span><span data-offset-key="220d3a6246434594b642d9ec25a3fcb7:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">binding</span></span><span data-offset-key="220d3a6246434594b642d9ec25a3fcb7:2"> of a context to a function.</span></span>

<span data-key="98687039118846a7aa3469c6fa62c8f0"><span data-offset-key="98687039118846a7aa3469c6fa62c8f0:0">From the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_objects/Function/bind" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406" data-rnw-int-class="257-15655_259-15656-237__"><span data-key="3fac0f38f77b4a94bbbb95bdea2a60dc"><span data-offset-key="3fac0f38f77b4a94bbbb95bdea2a60dc:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">Function.prototype.bind()</span></span></span></span></a><span data-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828"><span data-offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:0">, "The simplest use of </span><span data-offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind()</span></span><span data-offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:2"> is to make a function that, no matter how it is called, is called with a particular </span><span data-offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:4"> value".</span></span>

<span data-key="439fe46a014f4ce7a45646c852e57850"><span data-offset-key="439fe46a014f4ce7a45646c852e57850:0">Here is a preview of the syntax we use to </span><span data-offset-key="439fe46a014f4ce7a45646c852e57850:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="439fe46a014f4ce7a45646c852e57850:2">:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204"><span data-offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">let</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> aboundFunc </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">func</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">.</span></span></span></span><span Copied!

<span data-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1"><span data-offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:0">So when we call </span><span data-offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:2"> we are returned what is called an exotic function. Which essentially means a function with it's </span><span data-offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:4"> bound no matter where that function is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-key="33656168e80b402e86df0729c35bd829"><span data-offset-key="33656168e80b402e86df0729c35bd829:0">Let's take a look at example at </span><span data-offset-key="33656168e80b402e86df0729c35bd829:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="33656168e80b402e86df0729c35bd829:2"> in action:</span></span>

<span data-key="e4d7001f8df64a6d9285987040e70c87"><span data-offset-key="e4d7001f8df64a6d9285987040e70c87:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">boundCat</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e4d7001f8df64a6d9285987040e70c87:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e4d7001f8df64a6d9285987040e70c87:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e4d7001f8df64a6d9285987040e70c87:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e4d7001f8df64a6d9285987040e70c87:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="e4d7001f8df64a6d9285987040e70c87:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// prints "meow"</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9"><span data-offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:0">That is the magic of </span><span data-offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">Function\#bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:2">! It allows you choose the context for your function. You don't need to restrict the context you'd like to bind to either - you can </span><span data-offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:4"> functions to any context.</span></span>

<span data-key="55ba1214c0cb402ea9cd8c11c724f28e"><span data-offset-key="55ba1214c0cb402ea9cd8c11c724f28e:0">Let's look at another example:</span></span>

<span data-key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207"><span data-offset-key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207:0">So far we've talking of one of the the common uses of the </span><span data-offset-key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207:2"> function - binding a context to a function. <span data-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3"><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:0">Note that in the above snippet where we </span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:2"> with </span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">null</span></span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:4"> we donâ€™t actually use </span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:6"> in the </span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">sum</span></span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:8"> function. However, since </span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:10"> requires a first argument we can put in </span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">null</span></span><span data-offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:12"> as a place holder.</span></span>

<span data-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b"><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:0">Above when we created the </span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">add3</span></span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:2"> function we were creating a new bound function where the context was </span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">null</span></span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:4">, since the context won't matter, and the first argument will </span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">always</span></span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:6"> be </span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">3</span></span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:8"> for that function. Whenever we invoke the </span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">add3</span></span><span data-offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:10"> function all other arguments will be passed in normally.</span></span>

<span data-key="59ceb35e496c4b05a0322bdd576ed85a"><span data-offset-key="59ceb35e496c4b05a0322bdd576ed85a:0">Using </span><span data-offset-key="59ceb35e496c4b05a0322bdd576ed85a:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">bind</span></span><span data-offset-key="59ceb35e496c4b05a0322bdd576ed85a:2"> like this gives you a lot of flexibility with your code. Allowing you to create independent functions that essentially do the same thing while keeping your code very DRY.</span></span>

<span data-key="389fe6c3fd8544d5821f03d63bf0655a"><span data-offset-key="389fe6c3fd8544d5821f03d63bf0655a:0">Here is another example:</span></span>

data-offset-key="d4c4d84ce2d2474ca4d5be391ada8992:10"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span Copied!

<span data-key="eeecb1d85dbc452ab5d77cbd4eddd280"><span data-offset-key="eeecb1d85dbc452ab5d77cbd4eddd280:0">How to define a method that references </span><span data-offset-key="eeecb1d85dbc452ab5d77cbd4eddd280:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="eeecb1d85dbc452ab5d77cbd4eddd280:2"> on an object</span></span>

<span data-key="e550d3270d184d53bd1cb1b8f698ccc1"><span data-offset-key="e550d3270d184d53bd1cb1b8f698ccc1:0">Arrow Functions</span></span>

<span data-key="add7f71221e34205b784e20b3e1da9c9"><span data-offset-key="add7f71221e34205b784e20b3e1da9c9:0">Arrow functions, a.k.a. Fat Arrows (</span><span data-offset-key="add7f71221e34205b784e20b3e1da9c9:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">=&gt;</span></span><span data-offset-key="add7f71221e34205b784e20b3e1da9c9:2">), are a more concise way of declaring functions. Arrow functions were introduced in ES2015 as a way of solving many of the inconveniences of the normal callback function syntax.</span></span>

<span data-key="99981db90dbd40a98d1b502c38d2da62"><span data-offset-key="99981db90dbd40a98d1b502c38d2da62:0">Two major factors influenced the reason behind the desire for arrow functions: the need for shorter functions and behavior of </span><span data-offset-key="99981db90dbd40a98d1b502c38d2da62:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="99981db90dbd40a98d1b502c38d2da62:2"> and context.</span></span>

<span data-key="7a94a317ce1f44b9a1eb9232bf907a85"><span data-offset-key="7a94a317ce1f44b9a1eb9232bf907a85:0">When you finish this reading you should be able to:</span></span>

<span data-key="0ed04afa9a8b48fe8d99899d35bfd422"><span data-offset-key="0ed04afa9a8b48fe8d99899d35bfd422:0">Arrow functions solving problems</span></span>

<span data-key="98d9723a38cf4460a86edfc30ba0739f"><span data-offset-key="98d9723a38cf4460a86edfc30ba0739f:0">Let's start by looking at the arrow function in action!</span></span>

<span data-key="9ccee4e44b8d44408ced107915fa42e3"><span data-offset-key="9ccee4e44b8d44408ced107915fa42e3:0">Both functions in the example above accomplish the same thing. However, the arrow syntax is a little shorter and easier to follow.</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="cf1cbbc2fb024acdb092cfd78d7b8dfa"><span data-offset-key="cf1cbbc2fb024acdb092cfd78d7b8dfa:0">Anatomy of an arrow function</span></span>

<span data-key="3e4c625128d4429fb92d4d814686aa94"><span data-offset-key="3e4c625128d4429fb92d4d814686aa94:0">The syntax for a multiple statement arrow function is as follows:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="1a111a5b34b34bc9911ea7a42cebf9e6"><span data-offset-key="1a111a5b34b34bc9911ea7a42cebf9e6:0">(parameters, go, here) =&gt; {</span></span>

2

<span data-key="4826c3e497b74033a8aee90423b7c8a8"><span data-offset-key="4826c3e497b74033a8aee90423b7c8a8:0"> statement1;</span></span>

3

<span data-key="b4c4e43e8b9a414f82522c8ec8ae104e"><span data-offset-key="b4c4e43e8b9a414f82522c8ec8ae104e:0"> statement2;</span></span>

4

<span data-key="3ca2a4f9f4164915ae0ea86eff759deb"><span data-offset-key="3ca2a4f9f4164915ae0ea86eff759deb:0"> return &lt;a value&gt;;</span></span>

5

<span data-key="cc3731aac9bc4c0e868b0979fa5c0d29"><span data-offset-key="cc3731aac9bc4c0e868b0979fa5c0d29:0">}</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b"><span data-offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:0">So let's look at a quick translation between a function declared with a function expression syntax and a fat arrow function. Take notice of the removal of the </span><span data-offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">function</span></span><span data-offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:2"> keyword, and the addition of the fat arrow (</span><span data-offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">=&gt;</span></span><span data-offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:4">).</span></span>

1

<span data-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90"><span data-offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span <span data-key="f3127a444790429dbd52ceb16ecc6ff9"><span data-offset-key="f3127a444790429dbd52ceb16ecc6ff9:0">If there is only a single parameter you may omit the </span><span data-offset-key="f3127a444790429dbd52ceb16ecc6ff9:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">( )</span></span><span data-offset-key="f3127a444790429dbd52ceb16ecc6ff9:2"> around the parameter declaration:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="428ccaf286d9447baa10178a8141855b"><span data-offset-key="428ccaf286d9447baa10178a8141855b:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">param1</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="428ccaf286d9447baa10178a8141855b:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="428ccaf286d9447baa10178a8141855b:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=&gt;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="428ccaf286d9447baa10178a8141855b:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="428ccaf286d9447baa10178a8141855b:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="9d31b53208dd48918f68dc7c339e69fb"><span data-offset-key="9d31b53208dd48918f68dc7c339e69fb:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Single expression arrow functions</span></span></span>

<span data-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0"><span data-offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">Reminder:</span></span><span data-offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:1"> In JavaScript, an </span><span data-offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">expression</span></span><span data-offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:3"> is a line of code that returns a value. </span><span data-offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">Statements</span></span><span data-offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:5"> are, more generally, any line of code.</span></span>

<span data-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057"><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:0">One of the most fun things about single expression arrow functions is they allow for something previously unavailable in JavaScript: </span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">implicit returns</span></span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:2">. Meaning, in an arrow function with a single-expression block, the curly braces (</span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">{ }</span></span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:4">) and the </span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">return</span></span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:6"> are keyword are </span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">implied</span></span><span data-offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:8">.</span></span>

1

<span data-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950"><span data-offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">argument</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=&gt;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> expression</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// equal to (argument) =&gt; { return expression };</span></span></span></span></span>
