<span data-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a"><span data-offset-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">sayHello</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"Curtis"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="ea5be4503f9a457dab523691e53a5d5a:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-aa0ob8">// =&gt; Hi, Curtis</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="e2129cec27c84967893675ded556ca76"><span data-offset-key="e2129cec27c84967893675ded556ca76:0">That's about all you need to know for arrow functions syntax-wise. Arrow functions aren't just a different way of writing functions, though. They </span><span data-offset-key="e2129cec27c84967893675ded556ca76:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">behave</span></span><span data-offset-key="e2129cec27c84967893675ded556ca76:2"> differently too - especially when it comes to context!</span></span>

<span data-key="7b0ab2ce05c74f4ab429132d155cddf7"><span data-offset-key="7b0ab2ce05c74f4ab429132d155cddf7:0">Arrow functions with context</span></span>

<span data-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6"><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:0">Arrow functions, unlike normal functions, </span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">carry over context, binding </span></span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span></span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q"> lexically</span></span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:4">. In other words, </span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:6"> means the same thing inside an arrow function that it does outside of it. Unlike all other functions, the value of </span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:8"> inside an arrow function is not dependent on how it is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-key="91e31858a9634e6d8dc79db556ca9192"><span data-offset-key="91e31858a9634e6d8dc79db556ca9192:0">Let's do a little compare and contrast to illustrate this point:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="2e89e063edb449c5891a9d4cb38f6f9d"><span data-offset-key="2e89e063edb449c5891a9d4cb38f6f9d:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">const</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="2e89e063edb449c5891a9d4cb38f6f9d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> testObj </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="2e89e063edb449c5891a9d4cb38f6f9d:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="2e89e063edb449c5891a9d4cb38f6f9d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="2e89e063edb449c5891a9d4cb38f6f9d:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

2

<span data-key="b4623af55c024935a1a8dfb3a8c48af7"><span data-offset-key="b4623af55c024935a1a8dfb3a8c48af7:0"> name</span><span data-offset-key="b4623af55c024935a1a8dfb3a8c48af7:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">:</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b4623af55c024935a1a8dfb3a8c48af7:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b4623af55c024935a1a8dfb3a8c48af7:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-10pvkil">"The original object!"</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="b4623af55c024935a1a8dfb3a8c48af7:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">,</span></span></span></span></span>

3

<span data-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d"><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406">createFunc</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">:</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:4"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1190u7d">function</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="6b15c12570f94a00ad43dea5cb7c2b9d:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">{</span></span></span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef"><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:0">Let's walk through what just happened - we created a </span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">testObj</span></span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:2"> with two methods that each returned an anonymous function. The difference between these two methods is that the </span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">createArrowFunc</span></span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:4"> function contained an arrow function inside it. When we invoked both methods we created two function - the </span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">noName</span></span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:6"> function creating it's own scope and context while the </span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">arrowName</span></span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:8"> </span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:9"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-b88u0q">kept</span></span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:10"> the context of the function that created it (</span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:11"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">createArrowFunc</span></span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:12">'s context of </span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:13"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">testObj</span></span><span data-offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:14">).</span></span>

<span data-key="207a8bca7cbe4fadbf65afa487b6c17a"><span data-offset-key="207a8bca7cbe4fadbf65afa487b6c17a:0">An arrow function will always have the same context as the function that created it - giving it access to variables available in that context (like </span><span data-offset-key="207a8bca7cbe4fadbf65afa487b6c17a:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this.name</span></span><span data-offset-key="207a8bca7cbe4fadbf65afa487b6c17a:2"> in this case!)</span></span>

### 

<span data-key="c8ac4f24340446758da8ea813a442251"><span data-offset-key="c8ac4f24340446758da8ea813a442251:0">No binding in arrow functions</span></span>

<span data-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076"><span data-offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:0">One thing to know about arrow functions is since they already have a </span><span data-offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-36ujnk">bound context</span></span><span data-offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:2">, unlike normal functions, you can't reassign </span><span data-offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:4">. The </span><span data-offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">this</span></span><span data-offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:6"> in arrow functions is always what it was at the time that the arrow function was declared.</span></span>

1

<span data-key="e5c0338955764c708e08c9f1e247d81d"><span data-offset-key="e5c0338955764c708e08c9f1e247d81d:0">How to define an arrow function</span></span>

<span data-key="0c946072e0df485b9620f79fd6c129ab"><span data-offset-key="0c946072e0df485b9620f79fd6c129ab:0">Scope Problems</span></span>

<span data-key="df3d539b5930445383974a0ff94277fd"><span data-offset-key="df3d539b5930445383974a0ff94277fd:0">It's time to get some practice using scope in the wild! This task includes a link to download a </span><span data-offset-key="df3d539b5930445383974a0ff94277fd:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">zip</span></span><span data-offset-key="df3d539b5930445383974a0ff94277fd:2"> file with a number of problems.</span></span>

<span data-key="c661514add3c49cbad1e919fd3865287"><span data-offset-key="c661514add3c49cbad1e919fd3865287:0">Complete the problems in the order specified. In addition to the prompts available at the top of each file, Mocha specs are provided to test your work.</span></span>

<span data-key="0f267c6afb39419c9bbe339e7e3bf558"><span data-offset-key="0f267c6afb39419c9bbe339e7e3bf558:0">To get started, use the following commands:</span></span>

<span data-key="ca29930232f24a5497f757aca41c9fc9"><span data-offset-key="ca29930232f24a5497f757aca41c9fc9:0">WhiteBoarding Problem</span></span>

<span data-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d"><span data-offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:0">Write a function named </span><span data-offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:1"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">hiddenCounter()</span></span><span data-offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:2">. The </span><span data-offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">hiddenCounter</span></span><span data-offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:4"> function will start by declaring a variable that will keep track of a count and will be initially set to 0. Upon first invocation </span><span data-offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:5"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t">hiddenCounter</span></span><span data-offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:6"> will return a function. Every subsequent invocation will increment the previously described count variable.</span></span>

<span data-key="9eb924d08ece471a9f8278f6c618fee8"><span data-offset-key="9eb924d08ece471a9f8278f6c618fee8:0">Explain how the closure you have created affects the scope of both functions.</span></span>

<span data-key="2e13b12ef16b449f9c8f2a6cf6dd14d5"><span data-offset-key="2e13b12ef16b449f9c8f2a6cf6dd14d5:0">Examples:</span></span>

1

<span data-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0"><span data-offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:0"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> hidden1 </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:2"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-1wck8a6">=</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:3"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"> </span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:4"><span class="css-901oao class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">(</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:6"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">)</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:7"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406 r-cc4kyd">;</span></span></span></span><span data-offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:8"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span class="css-901oao css-16my406"><span
